JSON Schema Version Migration Pipeline\\n\\nThe Grafana dashboard migration system implements a comprehensive two-tier pipeline with parallel implementations in both Go (backend) and TypeScript (frontend) to ensure consistent schema versioning and dashboard transformation across the application.\\n\\n### Backend Migration Infrastructure (Go)\\n\\n**Migration Runner** (`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/migrate.go`):\\n- Provides the `Migrate()` function which is the main entry point for migrating dashboards\\n- Uses a singleton `migrator` struct that manages the migration pipeline\\n- `Initialize()` function sets up the migrator with data source information\\n- Orchestrates the full migration pipeline including frontend defaults application, panel ID management, schema version migrations, and cleanup operations\\n- The migration flow: cleanup → apply defaults → migrate versions → add annotations → cleanup for save\\n\\n**Migration Registry** (`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migrations.go`):\\n- `GetMigrations()` function returns a map[int]SchemaVersionMigrationFunc mapping version numbers to migration functions\\n- Maps versions 2-42 to individual migration functions (V2 through V42)\\n- Some migrations like V33 and V36 use closures to capture DataSourceInfoProvider for dynamic datasource lookups\\n- Latest version is 42 (marked as final for v1 dashboard API)\\n- `SchemaVersionMigrationFunc` type defines the signature for all migration functions: `func(context.Context, map[string]interface{}) error`\\n\\n**Individual Migration Steps**:\\n- V2 (`v2.go`): Migrates legacy services.filter structure to time and templating properties\\n- V16 (`v16.go`): Migrates dashboard layout from row-based system to modern grid-based layout\\n- V36 (`v36.go`): Converts datasource references from string format to structured UID-based objects\\n- V37-V42: Various panel and dashboard refinements\\n- V3-V15, V17-V35, V38-V41: Additional schema refinements and normalizations\\n\\n**Frontend Defaults Application** (`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/frontend_defaults.go`):\\n- `applyFrontendDefaults()`: Applies DashboardModel constructor defaults (title, tags, timezone, time range, etc.)\\n- `applyPanelDefaults()`: Applies PanelModel defaults to all panels (gridPos, targets with refId:A, fieldConfig, etc.)\\n- `cleanupDashboardForSave()`: Removes non-persisted properties and null values to match frontend's getSaveModel behavior\\n- `applyPanelAutoMigration()`: Handles auto-migration of legacy panel types (graph→timeseries, table-old→table, singlestat→stat, etc.)\\n- Manages panel ID uniqueness and grid position sorting\\n\\n**Utilities and Error Handling**:\\n- `migration_utils.go`: Provides helper functions for safe type conversions (GetStringValue, GetBoolValue, GetIntValue, GetFloatValue, ConvertToFloat, ConvertToInt)\\n- `errors.go`: Defines MigrationError and MinimumVersionError types for detailed error reporting\\n- `datasource_utils.go`: Provides datasource reference conversion utilities\\n\\n### Frontend Migration Implementation (TypeScript)\\n\\n**DashboardMigrator** (`public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardMigrator.ts`):\\n- `DashboardMigrator` class with `updateSchema()` method that mirrors the backend migration logic\\n- `DASHBOARD_SCHEMA_VERSION = 42` constant marking the final version (no new schema versions are added)\\n- Implements schema version migrations for v2-v42 with conditional blocks checking oldVersion < targetVersion\\n- Handles panel type migrations, datasource reference conversions, and field config transformations\\n- Imports specialized migration functions for CloudWatch metrics and annotations\\n\\n**DashboardModel** (`public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardModel.ts`):\\n- Main dashboard model class that instantiates DashboardMigrator\\n- Manages schemaVersion property and handles default values\\n- Integrates with PanelModel for panel-level migrations\\n- Supports targetSchemaVersion parameter for single-version migrations\\n\\n**PanelModel** (`public/app/features/dashboard/state/PanelModel.ts`):\\n- Panel-level model with auto-migration logic for legacy panel types\\n- Handles panel plugin type mapping and field config management\\n- Works in conjunction with getPanelPluginToMigrateTo for determining target panel types\\n\\n**Panel Type Migration** (`public/app/features/dashboard/state/getPanelPluginToMigrateTo.ts`):\\n- `getPanelPluginToMigrateTo()` function determines which panel plugin type legacy panels should migrate to\\n- Handles graph panel special logic (migrates to timeseries by default, bargauge or barchart based on xaxis mode, histogram for histogram mode)\\n- Maps deprecated panel types: table-old→table, singlestat→stat, grafana-singlestat-panel→stat, grafana-piechart-panel→piechart, grafana-worldmap-panel→geomap, natel-discrete-panel→state-timeline\\n\\n### Testing Infrastructure\\n\\n**Test Files**:\\n- Individual version test files (`v2_test.go` through `v42_test.go`) verify each migration step\\n- `DashboardMigrator.test.ts`: Frontend migration tests validating the TypeScript implementation\\n- `DashboardMigratorToBackend.test.ts`: Comprehensive comparison tests ensuring backend and frontend migration produce identical results\\n- Test data includes 40+ curated dashboard JSON files covering various schema versions and scenarios\\n\\n**Documentation**:\\n- `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/README.md`: Comprehensive guide covering:\\n  - Migration architecture and design patterns\\n  - How to add new migrations (now discouraged - new panel migrations should be done at plugin level)\\n  - Frontend and backend implementation details\\n  - Testing strategies including single-version and full-pipeline tests\\n  - Dataset coverage spanning v14-v42\\n\\n### Architecture Highlights\\n\\n1. **Parallel Implementation**: Both backend (Go) and frontend (TypeScript) implement the exact same logic to ensure consistency\\n2. **Stateless Migrations**: Each migration step is a pure function operating on the dashboard object\\n3. **Version Sequencing**: Migrations are applied sequentially from current version to target version\\n4. **Schema Versioning**: Version 42 is final - no new schema versions are added; panel-specific migrations are handled by panel plugins\\n5. **Datasource Handling**: V33 and V36 migrations require datasource information, using DataSourceInfoProvider interface\\n6. **Default Values Management**: Frontend defaults are applied before migrations to ensure consistent behavior\\n7. **Cleanup Phase**: Post-migration cleanup removes non-persisted properties and null values to match save model behavior\\n\\nThe system successfully bridges frontend and backend implementations, ensuring that dashboards JSON Schema Version Migration Pipeline\\n\\nThe Grafana dashboard migration system implements a comprehensive two-tier pipeline with parallel implementations in both Go (backend) and TypeScript (frontend) to ensure consistent schema versioning and dashboard transformation across the application.\\n\\n### Backend Migration Infrastructure (Go)\\n\\n**Migration Runner** (`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/migrate.go`):\\n- Provides the `Migrate()` function which is the main entry point for migrating dashboards\\n- Uses a singleton `migrator` struct that manages the migration pipeline\\n- `Initialize()` function sets up the migrator with data source information\\n- Orchestrates the full migration pipeline including frontend defaults application, panel ID management, schema version migrations, and cleanup operations\\n- The migration flow: cleanup → apply defaults → migrate versions → add annotations → cleanup for save\\n\\n**Migration Registry** (`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migrations.go`):\\n- `GetMigrations()` function returns a map[int]SchemaVersionMigrationFunc mapping version numbers to migration functions\\n- Maps versions 2-42 to individual migration functions (V2 through V42)\\n- Some migrations like V33 and V36 use closures to capture DataSourceInfoProvider for dynamic datasource lookups\\n- Latest version is 42 (marked as final for v1 dashboard API)\\n- `SchemaVersionMigrationFunc` type defines the signature for all migration functions: `func(context.Context, map[string]interface{}) error`\\n\\n**Individual Migration Steps**:\\n- V2 (`v2.go`): Migrates legacy services.filter structure to time and templating properties\\n- V16 (`v16.go`): Migrates dashboard layout from row-based system to modern grid-based layout\\n- V36 (`v36.go`): Converts datasource references from string format to structured UID-based objects\\n- V37-V42: Various panel and dashboard refinements\\n- V3-V15, V17-V35, V38-V41: Additional schema refinements and normalizations\\n\\n**Frontend Defaults Application** (`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/frontend_defaults.go`):\\n- `applyFrontendDefaults()`: Applies DashboardModel constructor defaults (title, tags, timezone, time range, etc.)\\n- `applyPanelDefaults()`: Applies PanelModel defaults to all panels (gridPos, targets with refId:A, fieldConfig, etc.)\\n- `cleanupDashboardForSave()`: Removes non-persisted properties and null values to match frontend's getSaveModel behavior\\n- `applyPanelAutoMigration()`: Handles auto-migration of legacy panel types (graph→timeseries, table-old→table, singlestat→stat, etc.)\\n- Manages panel ID uniqueness and grid position sorting\\n\\n**Utilities and Error Handling**:\\n- `migration_utils.go`: Provides helper functions for safe type conversions (GetStringValue, GetBoolValue, GetIntValue, GetFloatValue, ConvertToFloat, ConvertToInt)\\n- `errors.go`: Defines MigrationError and MinimumVersionError types for detailed error reporting\\n- `datasource_utils.go`: Provides datasource reference conversion utilities\\n\\n### Frontend Migration Implementation (TypeScript)\\n\\n**DashboardMigrator** (`public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardMigrator.ts`):\\n- `DashboardMigrator` class with `updateSchema()` method that mirrors the backend migration logic\\n- `DASHBOARD_SCHEMA_VERSION = 42` constant marking the final version (no new schema versions are added)\\n- Implements schema version migrations for v2-v42 with conditional blocks checking oldVersion < targetVersion\\n- Handles panel type migrations, datasource reference conversions, and field config transformations\\n- Imports specialized migration functions for CloudWatch metrics and annotations\\n\\n**DashboardModel** (`public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardModel.ts`):\\n- Main dashboard model class that instantiates DashboardMigrator\\n- Manages schemaVersion property and handles default values\\n- Integrates with PanelModel for panel-level migrations\\n- Supports targetSchemaVersion parameter for single-version migrations\\n\\n**PanelModel** (`public/app/features/dashboard/state/PanelModel.ts`):\\n- Panel-level model with auto-migration logic for legacy panel types\\n- Handles panel plugin type mapping and field config management\\n- Works in conjunction with getPanelPluginToMigrateTo for determining target panel types\\n\\n**Panel Type Migration** (`public/app/features/dashboard/state/getPanelPluginToMigrateTo.ts`):\\n- `getPanelPluginToMigrateTo()` function determines which panel plugin type legacy panels should migrate to\\n- Handles graph panel special logic (migrates to timeseries by default, bargauge or barchart based on xaxis mode, histogram for histogram mode)\\n- Maps deprecated panel types: table-old→table, singlestat→stat, grafana-singlestat-panel→stat, grafana-piechart-panel→piechart, grafana-worldmap-panel→geomap, natel-discrete-panel→state-timeline\\n\\n### Testing Infrastructure\\n\\n**Test Files**:\\n- Individual version test files (`v2_test.go` through `v42_test.go`) verify v14-v42\\n\\n### Architecture Highlights\\n\\n1. **Parallel Implementation**: Both backend (Go) and frontend (TypeScript) implement the exact same logic to ensure consistency\\n2. **Stateless Migrations**: Each migration step is a pure function operating on the dashboard object\\n3. **Version Sequencing**: Migrations are applied sequentially from current version to target version\\n4. **Schema Versioning**: Version 42 is final - no new schema versions are added; panel-specific migrations are handled by panel plugins\\n5. **Datasource Handling**: V33 and V36 migrations require datasource information, using DataSourceInfoProvider interface\\n6. **Default Values Management**: Frontend defaults are applied before migrations to ensure consistent behavior\\n7. **Cleanup Phase**: Post-migration cleanup removes non-persisted properties and null values to match save model behavior\\n\\nThe system successfully bridges frontend and backend implementations, ensuring that dashboards
